 Finally, after about 30 hours, the lifeline of Mumbai came to life
 ek hajaar se zyada hadataali motorman ne apana hadtaal khatm karne kaa elaan kar diya
 Perhaps both the government's strictness and the government's appeal played an important role in bringing Mumbai's lifeline back on track, but Mumbai's braking continued in these 30 hours
 kareeb 70 lakh musafiron kii mushkilon ko dekhte hue maharashtra sarkaar ko bhi harakat main aana hi padaa
 The state government had to impose ESMA on Mumbai's striking motorman
 mumbai main 150 motorman se zyada kii giraftaar hui

 shaayad isi kaa nateeja rahaa ki mumbai ke hadataali motorman ne shaam ke 5 bajane se pehle hi apni hadtaal waapas lene kaa elaan kar diya
 Here, in the Parliament in Delhi, 1,500 km from Mumbai, there was an echo of the uproar over the strike and it would not be wrong to say that the motorman also had its effect in the end of the strike
 shivasena or bijepi ke alaava duusare dalon ke netaaon ne bhi hadtaal ko lekar sarkaar par dabaav bananaa shuru kar diya tha
 Meanwhile, to end the strike in Mumbai itself, MNS chief Raj Thackeray warned the motormen to return to work by evening
 mumkin he ki raaj thakare kii dhamkee or emenes ke kaaryakartaaon ke hangaame se motorman bhi andolan waapas par majaboor ho gaye hon

 saaf he ki sarkaar kii sakhti or sarkaar kii apil donon ne motorman kii hadtaal ko khatm karne main bhoomika adaa kii

 JIPMER MBBS 2019:jawaharlal institute of postagraduate medical ajukeshan and research kii ore se yojit JIPMER pariksha 2 june ko he
 This year, a total of 1,84,272 candidates applied for the examination
 inamen se 94,073 students morning shift main or 90,199 students evening shift main pariksha denge
 This examination will be conducted in 280 centers
 pariksha ke nattejey 21 june ko yaa isse pehle jari kar die jaaenge
 The examination will be followed by first round counseling from 26 June to 28 June
 24 july ko second round counselling, 21 agast ko third round counselling or 26 sitambar ko final round counselling hogi
 subject-wise Marks - Physics - 60- Chemistry - 60- Biology - 60- English Language and Comprehension - 10- Logical and Quantitative Reasoning - 10JIPMER Candidates successful in MBBS exam can get admission in 200 seats in Puducherry and Karaikal
 yah course chaar saal or 6 maheene kaa hota he

 LG Candy kaa smartphone bharat main launch, keemat 6,699 rupee There is a special kind of temple at Rajnandgaon in Chhattisgarh
 yah mandir kisi devi-devtaa kaa nahin balkikutte kaahe
 a dog statue is installed in the temple
 mandir se judi yah manyata he ki iske pradakshina se kukur khaansee va kute ke kaatane se koi rog nahin hota
 The 'kukurdev Temple' is in Malighori Khapri village, six kilometers from Balod in Rajnandgaon
 yah mandir darasal bhairav smarak he, jo bhagwaan shiv ko samarpit he
 Shivalinga is installed in the sanctum sanctorum of this temple
 mandir ke shikhar ke chaaron ore diwaar par naagon kaa ankan kiya gaya he
 This temple, however, was built by the Phani Nagavanshi rulers in the 14th-15th centuries
 is mandir ke praangan main spasht lipiyukt shilaalekh bhi he, jis par banjaaron kii basti, chand-suraj or taron kii akruti bani hui he
 Statues of Rama Lakshmana and Shatrughan are also kept
 mandir ke praangan main kute kii pratimaa bhi sthapit he
 According to Jan Shruti, once there was a settlement of Banjaras
 malighori naam ke banjaare ke paas ek paaltu kutta tha
 Due to the famine, Banjare had to mortgage his beloved dog near Malguzar
 isi bich, malgujaar ke ghar chori ho gai
 The dog had seen the thieves hiding the stolen goods from Malguzar's house in a nearby pond
 subah kutta malgujaar ko chori kaa saamaan chhupaae sthaan par le gaya or malgujaar ko chori kaa saamaan bhi mil gaya
 Aware of the dog's loyalty, he wrote all the details in a paper and tied it around his neck and freed him to go to the real owner
 apane kute ko malgujaar ke ghar se lautakar aayaa dekhakar banjaare ne danda se peet-petakar kute ko maar daalaa
 After the dog died, he realized his mistake by seeing the letter tied around his neck and Banjare built Kukur Samadhi in the temple courtyard in memory of his beloved Swami devotee dog
 baad main kisi ne kute kii murti bhi sthapit kar di
 Even today, this place is famous as the Kukurdev Temple
 is mandir main vaise log bhi aate hai, jinhen kute ne kaat liya ho
 Although no one is treated here, it is believed that by coming here, that person is cured
 'kukurdev mandir' kaa board dekhakar kautuhalvash bhi log yahaan aate hai
 However, due to lack of proper maintenance, this temple is becoming dilapidated
